### Summary

P1 overlay injects guidance into the next gate instruction and records a supervisor_policy_overlay_snapshot event; P2 confines policy evolution to .supervisor/policy-overlay.yaml; P3 attributes trend rows to policy_overlay_hash+policy_proposal_id (schema v10 + Alembic 0004); P4 drafts exactly one rollback on regression without applying it (automatic_policy_mutation False, overlay bytes unchanged); P5 folds near-duplicate lessons, retires no-benefit lessons while retaining history, and runs a cadence-idempotent weekly P11 false-accept audit that emits no gate-advancing write. File ownership matches the accepted implementation_plan exactly (22 files). gate_authority remains 'unchanged' and all new event payloads are observational/advisory.
